posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:A very cost-effective hotel with new facilities and a grand lobby. It is equivalent to staying in a five-star hotel for the price of a three-star hotel. The hotel is within walking distance of Tangqi Ancient Town and Chaoshan. It feels that the geographical location belongs to the old city, and there is no large-scale business around. The hotel reception service is not different from the international brand management, but the details can be strengthened. In particular, smoking is not prohibited indoors. There are ashtrays at the elevator entrance on each floor. There are no no-smoking signs in the room. The smell of smoke will run into the room when sleeping in the middle of the night, which is a harassment to non-smokers. I remember that according to the law, smoking indoors in public places is not a fine of 500 yuan for individuals, and a fine of 3,000 to 10,000 yuan for operators. Why is Baoding Kaiyuan so open-minded? I still have a good impression of this hotel. Let me evaluate it. I give it all five stars, but smoking indoors in public places is a bit too much. I hope you will abide by the laws and regulations. For fire safety and the health of guests, set up smoking points at the entrance of the hotel and encourage guests to smoke in designated areas.

posted:Posted October 5, 2023
msg:First of all, I want to praise Xiaoxiang. The service is very enthusiastic. The room type was upgraded when checking in, and it was also thoughtfully arranged to a quieter floor and room type. When encountering small problems, they will actively solve them for you, instead of making excuses for you like some hotels. This will give a hotel a good first impression.
Back to the topic, a simple evaluation
Facilities: The facilities are ok, everything is there, and the transportation is convenient.
Hygiene: The details need to be strengthened, and there are some neglected aspects in cleaning, which is really not right for the standards of a star hotel.
Buffet dinner for two: It's just average. There are not many choices, but it's convenient. The hotel can solve a meal
Breakfast: There are few varieties. Suggestions for improvement
Service: The service staff are still quite friendly. When checking out, they also gave souvenirs. This is very good and will leave a good impression on customers.
Shortcomings and suggestions:
1. There are too few robots. At 9 o'clock, you have to wait for more than half an hour to get the takeaway. If the takeaway ordered by the customer cannot be left for a long time, then complaints are inevitable. The experience is not good. Later I learned that there is only one robot in the whole hotel. For a hotel of this size, it should not be. It is strongly recommended to increase it.
2. The wifi is unstable. There are cases where I can't receive the verification code and can't log in, and it often drops the line. It is not friendly to young people and business travelers. You can't tell customers that it's because of the large number of people. The experience is not good. It is strongly recommended to improve
